\DoxyCodeLine{01405\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ avoid\ changes\ for\ existing\ platforms,\ we\ restrict\ usage\ of\ intptr\_t\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01406\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ platforms\ where\ the\ size\ of\ a\ pointer\ is\ larger\ than\ the\ size\ of\ long.}}
